3476         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible annotation");
3477         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3478         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3479 
3480       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3481         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3482           classfile_parse_error(
3483             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3484         }
3485         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3486         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3487           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3488           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3489           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3490         }
3491         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3492 
3493       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3494         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3495           classfile_parse_error(
3496             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3497         }
3498         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3499         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3500 
3501         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3502         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3503         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3504 
3505       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3506         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3507           classfile_parse_error(
3508             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3509         }
3510         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3511         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3512           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3513           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3514           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3515         }
3516         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3517 
3518       } else {
3519         // Skip unknown attributes
3520         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3521       }
3522       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3523     } // End of attributes For loop
3524 
3525     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3526                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3527                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3528                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3529                                                         CHECK_0);
3530     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3531                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3532                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3533                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3534                                                              CHECK_0);
3535 
3536     RecordComponent* record_component =
3537       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3538                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3539                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3540     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3541   }  // End of component processing loop
3542 
3543   // Restore buffer's current position.
3544   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3545   return calculate_attr_size;
3546 }
3547 
3548 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3549   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3550 }
3551 
3552 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3553   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3554 
3555   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3556   check_property(
3557     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3558     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3559     signature_index, CHECK);
3560   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3561 }
3562 
3563 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3564                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3565                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3566                                                                   TRAPS) {
3567   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3568   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3569 
3570   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3571 
3572   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3573                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3574                      attribute_byte_length,
3575                      CHECK);
3576 
3577   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3578 
3579   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3580 
3581   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3582                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3583                      CHECK);
3584 
3585 
3586   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3587   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3588   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3589   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3590   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3591 
3592   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3593   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3594   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3595 
3596   Array<u2>* const operands =
3597     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3598 
3599   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3600   // pool if there is an error.
3601   cp->set_operands(operands);
3602 
3603   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3604   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3605 
3606   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3607     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3608     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3609 
3610     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3611     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3612     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3613     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3614     check_property(
3615       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3616       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3617       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3618       bootstrap_method_index,
3619       CHECK);
3620 
3621     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3622       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3623       CHECK);
3624 
3625     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3626     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3627 
3628     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3629     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3630       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3631       check_property(
3632         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3633         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3634         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3635         argument_index,
3636         CHECK);
3637       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3638     }
3639   }
3640   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3641                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3642                      CHECK);
3643 }
3644 
3645 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3646   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3647     _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3648     Arguments::enable_preview();
3649 }
3650 
3651 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3652                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3653                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3654                                                  TRAPS) {
3655   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3656   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3657   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3658 
3659   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3660   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3661   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3662   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3663   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3664   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3665   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3666   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3667   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3668   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3669   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3670   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3671   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3672   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3673   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3674   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3675   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3676   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3677   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3678   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3679   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3680   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3681   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3682   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3683   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3684   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3685   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3686   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3687   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3688   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3689   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3690   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3691 
3692   // Iterate over attributes
3693   while (attributes_count--) {
3694     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3695     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3696     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3697     check_property(
3698       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3699       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3700       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3701     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3702     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3703       // Check for SourceFile tag
3704       if (_need_verify) {
3705         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3706       }
3707       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3708         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3709       } else {
3710         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3711       }
3712       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3713     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3714       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3715       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3716           classfile_parse_error(
3717             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3718       }
3719       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3720       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3721     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3722       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3723       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3724         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3725       } else {
3726         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3727       }
3728       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3729       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3730       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3731     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3732       // Check for Synthetic tag
3733       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3734       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3735         classfile_parse_error(
3736           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3737           attribute_length, CHECK);
3738       }
3739       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3740     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3741       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3742       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3743         classfile_parse_error(
3744           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3745           attribute_length, CHECK);
3746       }
3747     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3748       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3749         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3750           classfile_parse_error(
3751             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3752         }
3753         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3754           classfile_parse_error(
3755             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3756             attribute_length, CHECK);
3757         }
3758         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3759       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3760         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3761           classfile_parse_error(
3762             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3763         }
3764         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3765         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3766         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3767         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3768         parse_annotations(cp,
3769                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3770                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3771                           parsed_annotations,
3772                           _loader_data,
3773                           _can_access_vm_annotations,
3774                           CHECK);
3775         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3776       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3777         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3778           classfile_parse_error(
3779             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3780         }
3781         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3782         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3783           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3784           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3785           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3786         }
3787         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3788       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3789         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3790           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3791         } else {
3792           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3793         }
3794         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3795           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3796           attribute_length, CHECK);
3797         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3798         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3799         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3800         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3801           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3802         }
3803         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3804         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3805           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3806         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3807             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3808              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3809           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3810         }
3811       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3812                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3813         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3814           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3815         }
3816         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3817         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3818       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3819         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3820           classfile_parse_error(
3821             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3822         }
3823         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3824         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3825         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3826         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3827         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3828       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3829         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3830           classfile_parse_error(
3831             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3832         } else {
3833           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3834         }
3835         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3836           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3837           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3838           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3839         }
3840         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3841       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3842         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3843           // Check for NestMembers tag
3844           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3845             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3846           } else {
3847             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3848           }
3849           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3850             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3851           }
3852           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3853           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3854           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3855         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3856           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3857             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3858           } else {
3859             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3860           }
3861           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3862             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3863           }
3864           if (_need_verify) {
3865             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3866           }
3867           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3868           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3869           check_property(
3870                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3871                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3872                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3873           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3874         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3875           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3876             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3877             // not java.lang.Record.
3878             if (supports_records() &&
3879                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3880               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3881                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3882               }
3883               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3884               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3885                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3886               }
3887               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3888               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3889               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3890             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3891               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3892               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3893               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3894               // exception would have been thrown.
3895               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3896               if (supports_records()) {
3897                 log_info(class, record)(
3898                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3899                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3900               } else {
3901                 log_info(class, record)(
3902                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3903                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3904               }
3905             }
3906             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3907           } else {
3908             // Unknown attribute
3909             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3910           }
3911         } else {
3912           // Unknown attribute
3913           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3914         }
3915       } else {
3916         // Unknown attribute
3917         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3918       }
3919     } else {
3920       // Unknown attribute
3921       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3922     }
3923   }
3924   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3925                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3926                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3927                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3928                                             CHECK);
3929   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3930                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3931                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3932                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3933                                                  CHECK);
3934 
3935   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3936     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3937                             cfs,
3938                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3939                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3940                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3941                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3942                             CHECK);
3943     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3944       guarantee_property(
3945         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3946         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3947     }
3948   }
3949 
3950   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3951     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
3952                             cfs,
3953                             nest_members_attribute_start,
3954                             CHECK);
3955     if (_need_verify) {
3956       guarantee_property(
3957         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3958         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3959     }
3960   }
3961 
3962   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3963     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
3964                             cfs,
3965                             cp,
3966                             record_attribute_start,
3967                             CHECK);
3968     if (_need_verify) {
3969       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
3970                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
3971                          CHECK);
3972     }
3973   }
3974 
3975   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
3976     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
3977                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3978   }
3979 }
3980 
3981 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
3982   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
3983 
3984   if (_synthetic_flag)
3985     k->set_is_synthetic();
3986   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
3987     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
3988   }
3989   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3990     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
3991   }
3992   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
3993     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
3994   }
3995 }
3996 
3997 // Create the Annotations object that will
3998 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
3999 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
4000     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
4001         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
4002         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
4003         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
4004       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
4005       return;
4006     }
4007 
4008     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
4009     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
4010     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
4011     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
4012     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
4013 
4014     // This is the Annotations object that will be
4015     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4016     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4017 
4018     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4019     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4020     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4021     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4022     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4023     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4024 }
4025 
4026 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4027 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4028                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4029                                             int java_fields_count,
4030                                             TRAPS) {
4031   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4032 
4033   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4034   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4035   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4036   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4037   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4038   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4039   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4040   this_klass->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
4041   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4042   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4043   // Delay the setting of _transitive_interfaces until after initialize_supers() in
4044   // fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4045   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4046   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4047   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4048   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4049 
4050   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4051   clear_class_metadata();
4052 }
4053 
4054 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4055                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4056                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4057                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4058                                                        TRAPS) {
4059   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4060   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4061       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4062     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4063                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4064                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4065                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4066     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4067       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4068         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4069       }
4070     }
4071     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4072       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4073         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4074         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4075       }
4076     }
4077   }
4078   return annotations;
4079 }
4080 
4081 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4082                                                         const int super_class_index,
4083                                                         const bool need_verify,
4084                                                         TRAPS) {
4085   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4086   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4087 
4088   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4089     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4090                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_VALUE),
4091                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4092                    super_class_index,
4093                    CHECK_NULL);
4094   } else {
4095     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4096                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4097                    super_class_index,
4098                    CHECK_NULL);
4099     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4100     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4101     bool is_array = false;
4102     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4103       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4104       if (need_verify)
4105         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4106     } else if (need_verify) {
4107       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4108     }
4109     if (need_verify) {
4110       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4111                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4112     }
4113   }
4114   return super_klass;
4115 }
4116 
4117 #ifndef PRODUCT
4118 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4119                                Array<u2>* fields,
4120                                ConstantPool* cp,
4121                                int instance_size,
4122                                int instance_fields_start,
4123                                int instance_fields_end,
4124                                int static_fields_end) {
4125 
4126   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4127 
4128   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4129   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4130   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4131     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4132       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4133         fs.offset(),
4134         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4135         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4136     }
4137   }
4138   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4139   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4140   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4141   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4142     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4143       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4144         fs.offset(),
4145         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4146         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4147     }
4148   }
4149   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4150   tty->print("\n");
4151 }
4152 #endif
4153 
4154 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4155   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4156   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4157   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4158     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4159   } else {
4160     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4161         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4162     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4163   }
4164 }
4165 
4166 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4167   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4168   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4169 }
4170 
4171 // addition of super oop maps
4172 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4173   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4174          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4175 
4176   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4177   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4178 }
4179 
4180 // collection of oops
4181 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4182   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4183     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4184   }
4185   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4186   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4187     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4188     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4189   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4190     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4191   } else { // Need a new one...
4192     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4193     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4194     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4195     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4196     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4197   }
4198 }
4199 
4200 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4201 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4202   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4203     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4204   }
4205 }
4206 
4207 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4208 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4209   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4210     return;
4211   }
4212   /*
4213    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4214    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4215    * containing refs.
4216    *
4217    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4218    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4219    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4220    */
4221   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4222         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4223   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4224     return;
4225   }
4226 
4227   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4228   ResourceMark rm;
4229   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4230       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4231   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4232   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4233   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4234   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4235   oop_maps_copy++;
4236   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4237     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4238     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4239       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4240     } else {
4241       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4242       new_count++;
4243       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4244       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4245     }
4246     oop_maps_copy++;
4247   }
4248   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4249   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4250 }
4251 
4252 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4253   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4254   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4255     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4256     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4257     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4258     while (map <= last_map) {
4259       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4260                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4261       map++;
4262     }
4263   }
4264 }
4265 
4266 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4267   print_on(st);
4268 }
4269 
4270 void ClassFileParser::throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4271                                                 const char* msg,
4272                                                 const Symbol* name,
4273                                                 const Symbol* sig) const {
4274 
4275   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4276   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4277     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4278         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4279         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4280   }
4281   else {
4282     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4283         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4284         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4285         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4286   }
4287 }
4288 
4289 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4290 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4291                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4292                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4293                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4294                                     TRAPS) {
4295 
4296   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4297 
4298   // Field size and offset computation
4299   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4300                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4301   int next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4302   int first_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4303 
4304   // Fields that are inline types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4305   // - static fields are oops
4306   // - non-static fields are embedded
4307 
4308   // Count the contended fields by type.
4309   //
4310   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4311   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4312   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4313   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4314   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4315     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4316     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4317       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4318       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4319         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4320       }
4321     }
4322   }
4323 
4324 
4325   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4326   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4327   // Inline types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4328   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4329                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]) * heapOopSize);
4330   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4331     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4332   }
4333 
4334   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4335                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4336   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4337                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4338   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4339                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4340 
4341   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4342                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4343 
4344   // First field of inline types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4345   // in-lining of inline types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4346   // flatten inline types
4347   int initial_inline_type_padding = 0;
4348   if (is_inline_type()) {
4349     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4350     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4351     initial_inline_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4352   }
4353 
4354   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4355 
4356   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4357 
4358   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4359   if (is_contended_class) {
4360     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4361   }
4362 
4363   // Temporary inline types restrictions
4364   if (is_inline_type()) {
4365     if (is_contended_class) {
4366       throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4367       return;
4368     }
4369   }
4370 
4371   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4372   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4373   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4374   // exempt from that.
4375   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4376   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4377   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4378   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4379   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4380 
4381   int static_inline_type_count = 0;
4382   int nonstatic_inline_type_count = 0;
4383   int* nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NULL;
4384   Klass** nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NULL;
4385   unsigned int inline_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4386   int not_flattened_inline_types = 0;
4387   int not_atomic_inline_types = 0;
4388 
4389   int max_nonstatic_inline_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE] + 1;
4390 
4391   nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4392                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4393   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_inline_type; i++) {
4394     nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4395   }
4396   nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4397                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4398 
4399   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4400     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4401       ResourceMark rm;
4402       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4403         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4404       }
4405       static_inline_type_count++;
4406     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4407       // Pre-resolve the flattenable field and check for inline type circularity issues.
4408       ResourceMark rm;
4409       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4410         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4411       }
4412       Klass* klass =
4413         SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
4414                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4415                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4416       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4417       if (!klass->access_flags().is_inline_type()) {
4418         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4419       }
4420       ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4421       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4422       bool too_big_to_flatten = (InlineFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4423                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > InlineFieldMaxFlatSize);
4424       bool too_atomic_to_flatten = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4425       bool too_volatile_to_flatten = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4426       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4427         too_atomic_to_flatten = false;
4428         //too_volatile_to_flatten = false; //FIXME
4429         // volatile fields are currently never flattened, this could change in the future
4430       }
4431       if (!(too_big_to_flatten | too_atomic_to_flatten | too_volatile_to_flatten)) {
4432         nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = fs.index();
4433         nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = klass;
4434         nonstatic_inline_type_count++;
4435 
4436         ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4437         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4438           inline_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4439         }
4440         fs.set_flattened(true);
4441         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4442           not_atomic_inline_types++;
4443         }
4444       } else {
4445         not_flattened_inline_types++;
4446         fs.set_flattened(false);
4447       }
4448     }
4449   }
4450 
4451   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account not flattened inline types;
4452   nonstatic_oop_count += not_flattened_inline_types;
4453 
4454   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4455   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4456                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4457                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE];
4458 
4459   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4460           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4461   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4462     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4463   const bool has_nonstatic_value_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4464 
4465   if (is_inline_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4466     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4467     throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4468     return;
4469   }
4470 
4471   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4472   //
4473   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4474   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4475   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4476   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4477   // distinct regions.
4478   //
4479   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4480   int max_oop_map_count =
4481       super_oop_map_count +
4482       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4483       inline_type_oop_map_count +
4484       not_flattened_inline_types;
4485 
4486   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4487   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4488     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4489                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4490   }
4491 
4492   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4493 
4494   bool compact_fields  = true;
4495   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4496 
4497   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4498   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4499 
4500   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4501   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4502     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4503     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4504     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4505                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4506   } else {
4507     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4508     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4509   }
4510 
4511   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4512   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4513   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4514   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4515   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4516   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4517   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4518   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4519 
4520   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4521   // long/double alignment.
4522   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4523     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4524     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4525     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4526       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4527       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4528       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4529       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4530       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4531         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4532         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4533         length -= BytesPerInt;
4534         offset += BytesPerInt;
4535       }
4536       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4537       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4538         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4539         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4540         length -= BytesPerShort;
4541         offset += BytesPerShort;
4542       }
4543       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4544       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4545         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4546         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4547         length -= 1;
4548       }
4549       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4550       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4551       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4552           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4553         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4554         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4555         length -= heapOopSize;
4556         offset += heapOopSize;
4557       }
4558     }
4559   }
4560 
4561   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4562                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4563   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4564                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4565   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4566                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4567   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4568                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4569 
4570   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4571   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4572     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4573     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4574       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4575     }
4576     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4577   }
4578 
4579   // Aligning embedded inline types
4580   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded inline types always put them at the
4581   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4582   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4583   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each inline type starting on a
4584   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4585   // align inline types according to their most constrained internal type.
4586   next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4587   int next_inline_type_index = 0;
4588 
4589   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4590   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4591   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4592   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4593 
4594     // skip already laid out fields
4595     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4596 
4597     // contended instance fields are handled below
4598     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4599 
4600     int real_offset = 0;
4601     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4602 
4603     // pack the rest of the fields
4604     switch (atype) {
4605       // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4606       case STATIC_FLATTENABLE:   // Fallthrough
4607       case STATIC_OOP:
4608         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4609         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4610         break;
4611       case STATIC_BYTE:
4612         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4613         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4614         break;
4615       case STATIC_SHORT:
4616         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4617         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4618         break;
4619       case STATIC_WORD:
4620         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4621         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4622         break;
4623       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4624         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4625         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4626         break;
4627       case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4628         if (fs.is_flattened()) {
4629           Klass* klass = nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[next_inline_type_index];
4630           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4631           assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(),"Must be an inline type");
4632           ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4633           real_offset = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4634           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4635           // aligning next inline type on a 64 bits boundary
4636           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset, BytesPerLong);
4637           next_inline_type_index += 1;
4638 
4639           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4640             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4641             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4642             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4643             while (map < last_map) {
4644               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4645               map++;
4646             }
4647           }
4648           break;
4649         } else {
4650           // Fall through
4651         }
4652       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4653         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4654           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4655           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4656           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4657         } else {
4658           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4659           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4660         }
4661         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4662         break;
4663       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4664         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4665           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4666           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4667           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4668         } else {
4669           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4670           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4671         }
4672         break;
4673       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4674         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4675           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4676           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4677           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4678         } else {
4679           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4680           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4681         }
4682         break;
4683       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4684         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4685           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4686           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4687           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4688         } else {
4689           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4690           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4691         }
4692         break;
4693       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4694         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4695         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4696         break;
4697       default:
4698         ShouldNotReachHere();
4699     }
4700     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4701   }
4702 
4703 
4704   // Handle the contended cases.
4705   //
4706   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4707   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4708   // the fields with full-width padding.
4709   //
4710   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4711   // for each field.
4712   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4713 
4714     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4715     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4716 
4717     // collect all contended groups
4718     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4719     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4720       // skip already laid out fields
4721       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4722 
4723       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4724         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4725       }
4726     }
4727 
4728     int current_group = -1;
4729     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4730 
4731       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4732 
4733         // skip already laid out fields
4734         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4735 
4736         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4737         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4738 
4739         // handle statics below
4740         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4741 
4742         int real_offset = 0;
4743         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4744 
4745         switch (atype) {
4746           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4747             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4748             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4749             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4750             break;
4751 
4752           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4753             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4754             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4755             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4756             break;
4757 
4758           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4759             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4760             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4761             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4762             break;
4763 
4764           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4765             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4766             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4767             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4768             break;
4769 
4770             // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4771           case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4772             throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4773                                       "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4774             return;
4775 
4776           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4777             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4778             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4779             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4780             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4781             break;
4782 
4783           default:
4784             ShouldNotReachHere();
4785         }
4786 
4787         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4788           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4789           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4790           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4791           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4792           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4793         }
4794 
4795         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4796       } // for
4797 
4798       // Start laying out the next group.
4799       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4800       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4801       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4802       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4803       if (current_group != 0) {
4804         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4805       }
4806     }
4807 
4808     // handle static fields
4809   }
4810 
4811   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4812   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4813   // and/or adjacent object.
4814   if (is_contended_class) {
4815     assert(!is_inline_type(), "@Contended not supported for inline types yet");
4816     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4817   }
4818 
4819   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4820   if (nonstatic_inline_type_count != 0) {
4821     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4822   } else {
4823     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4824   }
4825 
4826   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4827   if (is_inline_type()) {
4828     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4829       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4830     }
4831   }
4832   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4833   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4834   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4835 
4836   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4837                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4838   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4839                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4840 
4841   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4842 
4843   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4844          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4845          + initial_inline_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4846 
4847 
4848   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4849   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4850   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4851   // assert without actually having the fields.
4852   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4853          is_contended_class ||
4854          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4855 
4856   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4857   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4858 
4859 #ifndef PRODUCT
4860   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_inline_type()) ||
4861       (PrintInlineLayout && (is_inline_type() || has_nonstatic_value_fields))) {
4862     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4863           _fields,
4864           cp,
4865           instance_size,
4866           nonstatic_fields_start,
4867           nonstatic_fields_end,
4868           static_fields_end);
4869     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4870     tty->print("\n");
4871     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4872     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4873     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4874     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4875     tty->print_cr("---");
4876   }
4877 
4878 #endif
4879   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4880   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4881   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4882   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4883   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4884   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;

4885 
4886   // An inline type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4887   // that field is simple enough.
4888   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_inline_type() &&
4889                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4890                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4891                                 (not_atomic_inline_types == 0) &&
4892                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4893   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4894   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4895   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4896   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4897   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4898 }
4899 
4900 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4901   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4902 
4903   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4904 
4905   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4906   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4907   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4908     if (_has_finalizer ||
4909         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4910       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4911     }
4912   }
4913 
4914 #ifdef ASSERT
4915   bool f = false;
4916   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4917                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4918   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4919       f = true;
4920   }
4921 
4922   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4923   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4924   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4925   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4926     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4927   }
4928 #endif
4929 
4930   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4931   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
4932     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
4933       if (ik->is_value()) {
4934         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
4935         throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
4936         return;
4937       }
4938       ik->set_is_cloneable();
4939     }
4940   }
4941 
4942   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
4943   if (super == NULL) {
4944     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
4945     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4946   } else {
4947     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
4948         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
4949       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4950     }
4951 #ifdef ASSERT
4952     bool v = false;
4953     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
4954       const Method* const constructor =
4955         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
4956                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4957       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
4958         v = true;
4959       }
4960     }
4961     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
4962 #endif
4963   }
4964 
4965   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
4966   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
4967   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
4968   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
4969       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
4970       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
4971       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
4972     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
4973     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
4974     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
4975   }
4976 }
4977 
4978 bool ClassFileParser::supports_inline_types() const {
4979   // Inline types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
4980   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
4981 }
4982 
4983 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
4984 
4985 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
4986                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
4987   // iterate over new interfaces
4988   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
4989     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
4990     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
4991     // add new interface
4992     result->append_if_missing(e);
4993   }
4994 }
4995 
4996 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
4997                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
4998                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
4999                                                             TRAPS) {
5000   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
5001   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
5002 
5003   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
5004   int max_transitive_size = 0;
5005   int super_size = 0;
5006   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
5007   if (super != NULL) {
5008     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5009     max_transitive_size += super_size;
5010   }
5011   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
5012   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
5013   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5014     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5015     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5016   }
5017   // Finally add local interfaces
5018   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5019   // Construct array
5020   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5021     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5022     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5023   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5024     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5025     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5026     // The three lines below are commented to work around bug JDK-8245487
5027 //  } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5028 //    // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5029 //    return local_ifs;
5030   } else {
5031     ResourceMark rm;
5032     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5033 
5034     // Copy down from superclass
5035     if (super != NULL) {
5036       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5037     }
5038 
5039     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5040     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5041       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5042       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5043     }
5044     // Finally add local interfaces
5045     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5046 
5047     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5048     const int length = result->length();
5049     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5050 
5051     if (length == 1 && result->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
5052       return Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
5053     }
5054 
5055     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
5056       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5057     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5058       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5059       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5060       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5061     }
5062     return new_result;
5063   }
5064 }
5065 
5066 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5067   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5068   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5069 
5070   if (super != NULL) {
5071 
5072     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5073     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5074     // special reflection class loader
5075     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5076       assert(super->is_instance_klass(), "super is not instance klass");
5077       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5078       if (super_package != NULL &&
5079           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5080           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5081         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5082         Exceptions::fthrow(
5083           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5084           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5085           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5086           this_klass->external_name(),
5087           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5088           super->external_name());
5089         return;
5090       }
5091     }
5092 
5093     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5094       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5095     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5096       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5097       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5098                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5099                                                       vca_result);
5100       if (msg == NULL) {
5101         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5102         Exceptions::fthrow(
5103           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5104           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5105           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5106           this_klass->external_name(),
5107           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5108           super->external_name(),
5109           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5110           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5111           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5112       } else {
5113         // Add additional message content.
5114         Exceptions::fthrow(
5115           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
