5116           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5117           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5118           msg);
5119       }
5120     }
5121   }
5122 }
5123 
5124 
5125 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5126   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5127   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5128   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5129   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5130     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5131     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5132     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5133       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5134     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5135       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5136       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5137                                                       k,
5138                                                       vca_result);
5139       if (msg == NULL) {
5140         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5141         Exceptions::fthrow(
5142           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5143           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5144           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5145           this_klass->external_name(),
5146           k->external_name(),
5147           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5148           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5149           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5150       } else {
5151         // Add additional message content.
5152         Exceptions::fthrow(
5153           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5154           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5155           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5156           msg);
5157       }
5158     }
5159   }
5160 }
5161 
5162 
5163 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5164   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5165   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5166   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5167 
5168   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5169   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5170     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5171 
5172     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5173     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5174         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5175 
5176       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5177       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5178       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5179       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5180       while (k != NULL) {
5181         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5182         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5183           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5184           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5185           if (super_m == NULL) {
5186             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5187           }
5188 
5189           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5190               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5191             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5192             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5193                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5194                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5195                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5196                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5197             if (can_access) {
5198               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5199               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5200               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5201                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5202                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5203                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5204                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5205                                  name->as_C_string(),
5206                                  signature->as_C_string()
5207                                  );
5208               return;
5209             }
5210           }
5211 
5212           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5213           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5214           continue;
5215         }
5216 
5217         k = k->super();
5218       }
5219     }
5220   }
5221 }
5222 
5223 
5224 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5225 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5226   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5227   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5228   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5229   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5230 
5231   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5232     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5233     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5234     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5235       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5236       Exceptions::fthrow(
5237         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5238         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5239         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5240         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5241         this_klass->external_name()
5242       );
5243       return;
5244     }
5245   }
5246 }
5247 
5248 // utility methods for format checking
5249 
5250 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5251   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5252   const bool is_inline_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_VALUE) != 0;
5253   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5254   assert(supports_inline_types() || !is_inline_type, "JVM_ACC_VALUE should not be set");
5255   if (is_module) {
5256     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5257     Exceptions::fthrow(
5258       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5259       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5260       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5261       _class_name->as_C_string());
5262     return;
5263   }
5264 
5265   if (is_inline_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5266     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5267     Exceptions::fthrow(
5268       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5269       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5270       "Class modifier ACC_VALUE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5271       _class_name->as_C_string()
5272     );
5273   }
5274 
5275   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5276 
5277   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5278   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5279   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5280   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5281   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5282   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5283   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5284   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5285 
5286   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5287       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5288       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5289       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5290       (is_inline_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5291     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5292     const char* class_note = "";
5293     if (is_inline_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5294     Exceptions::fthrow(
5295       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5296       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5297       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5298       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5299     );
5300     return;
5301   }
5302 }
5303 
5304 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5305   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5306   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5307   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5308 
5309   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5310           (is_public && is_private) ||
5311           (is_protected && is_private));
5312 }
5313 
5314 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5315 //
5316 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5317 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5318 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5319 //
5320 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5321   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5322   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5323   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5324     Exceptions::fthrow(
5325       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5326       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5327       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5328       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5329     return;
5330   }
5331 
5332   if (major > max_version) {
5333     Exceptions::fthrow(
5334       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5335       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5336       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5337       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5338       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5339     return;
5340   }
5341 
5342   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5343     return;
5344   }
5345 
5346   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5347     if (major != max_version) {
5348       Exceptions::fthrow(
5349         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5350         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5351         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5352         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5353         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5354       return;
5355     }
5356 
5357     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5358       Exceptions::fthrow(
5359         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5360         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5361         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5362         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5363       return;
5364     }
5365 
5366   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5367     Exceptions::fthrow(
5368         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5369         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5370         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5371         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5372   }
5373 }
5374 
5375 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5376                                                    bool is_interface,
5377                                                    bool is_inline_type,
5378                                                    TRAPS) const {
5379   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5380 
5381   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5382   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5383   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5384   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5385   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5386   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5387   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5388   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5389   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5390 
5391   bool is_illegal = false;
5392 
5393   if (is_interface) {
5394     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5395         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5396         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5397       is_illegal = true;
5398     }
5399   } else { // not interface
5400     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5401       is_illegal = true;
5402     } else {
5403       if (is_inline_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5404         is_illegal = true;
5405       }
5406     }
5407   }
5408 
5409   if (is_illegal) {
5410     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5411     Exceptions::fthrow(
5412       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5413       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5414       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5415       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5416     return;
5417   }
5418 }
5419 
5420 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5421                                                     bool is_interface,
5422                                                     bool is_inline_type,
5423                                                     const Symbol* name,
5424                                                     TRAPS) const {
5425   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5426 
5427   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5428   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5429   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5430   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5431   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5432   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5433   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5434   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5435   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5436   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5437   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5438   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5439   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5440 
5441   bool is_illegal = false;
5442 
5443   const char* class_note = "";
5444 
5445   if (is_interface) {
5446     if (major_gte_8) {
5447       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5448       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5449       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5450       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5451       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5452           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5453           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5454           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5455           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5456           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5457           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5458           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5459           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5460         is_illegal = true;
5461       }
5462     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5463       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5464       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5465           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5466         is_illegal = true;
5467       }
5468     } else {
5469       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5470       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5471         is_illegal = true;
5472       }
5473     }
5474   } else { // not interface
5475     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5476       is_illegal = true;
5477     } else {
5478       if (is_initializer) {
5479         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5480             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5481           is_illegal = true;
5482         }
5483         if (!is_static && !is_inline_type) {
5484           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5485         } else if (is_static && is_inline_type) {
5486           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5487         } else {
5488           // but no other combinations are allowed
5489           is_illegal = true;
5490           class_note = (is_inline_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5491         }
5492       } else { // not initializer
5493         if (is_inline_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5494           is_illegal = true;
5495           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5496         } else {
5497           if (is_abstract) {
5498             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5499                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5500               is_illegal = true;
5501             }
5502           }
5503         }
5504       }
5505     }
5506   }
5507 
5508   if (is_illegal) {
5509     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5510     Exceptions::fthrow(
5511       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5512       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5513       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5514       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5515     return;
5516   }
5517 }
5518 
5519 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5520                                         int length,
5521                                         TRAPS) const {
5522   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5523   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5524     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5525   }
5526 }
5527 
5528 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5529 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5530 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5531 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5532 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5533 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5534 //
5535 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5536 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5537 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5538                                               unsigned int length,
5539                                               int type) {
5540   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5541   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5542     switch(*p) {
5543       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5544       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5545       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5546         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5547         return false;
5548       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5549         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5550         // unqualified name must not be empty
5551         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5552           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5553               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5554             return false;
5555           }
5556         } else {
5557           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5558         }
5559         break;
5560       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5561       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5562         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5563         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5564           return false;
5565         }
5566     }
5567   }
5568   return true;
5569 }
5570 
5571 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5572 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5573 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5574 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5575 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5576 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5577 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5578 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5579                                         bool slash_ok,
5580                                         unsigned int length) {
5581   const char* p;
5582   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5583   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5584 
5585   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5586     const char* old_p = p;
5587     jchar ch = *p;
5588     if (ch < 128) {
5589       p++;
5590       // quick check for ascii
5591       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5592         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5593         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5594         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5595         last_is_slash = false;
5596         continue;
5597       }
5598       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5599         if (last_is_slash) {
5600           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5601         }
5602         last_is_slash = true;
5603         continue;
5604       }
5605     }
5606     else {
5607       jint unicode_ch;
5608       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5609       p = tmp_p;
5610       last_is_slash = false;
5611       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5612       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5613       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5614       // return value
5615       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5616       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5617       JavaCallArguments args;
5618       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5619 
5620       if (not_first_ch) {
5621         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5622         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5623           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5624           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5625           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5626           &args,
5627           THREAD);
5628       } else {
5629         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5630         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5631           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5632           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5633           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5634           &args,
5635           THREAD);
5636       }
5637       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5638         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5639         return NULL;
5640       }
5641       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5642         continue;
5643       }
5644     }
5645     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5646   }
5647   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5648 }
5649 
5650 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5651 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5652 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5653 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5654 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5655 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5656                                                        bool void_ok,
5657                                                        unsigned int length,
5658                                                        TRAPS) const {
5659   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5660   while (length > 0) {
5661     switch (signature[0]) {
5662     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5663     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5664     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5665     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5666     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5667     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5668     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5669     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5670     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5671       return signature + 1;
5672     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VALUETYPE:
5673       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5674       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5675       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5676       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5677       //                                    CHECK_0);
5678       // }
5679       // fall through
5680     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5681     {
5682       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5683         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5684         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5685 
5686         // The next character better be a semicolon
5687         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5688           return p + 1;
5689         }
5690       }
5691       else {
5692         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5693         signature++;
5694         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5695         // Format check signature
5696         if (c != NULL) {
5697           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5698           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5699           if (!legal) {
5700             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5701                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5702                                   CHECK_NULL);
5703             return NULL;
5704           }
5705           return signature + newlen + 1;
5706         }
5707       }
5708       return NULL;
5709     }
5710     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5711       array_dim++;
5712       if (array_dim > 255) {
5713         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5714         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5715       }
5716       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5717       signature++;
5718       length--;
5719       void_ok = false;
5720       break;
5721     default:
5722       return NULL;
5723     }
5724   }
5725   return NULL;
5726 }
5727 
5728 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5729 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5730   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5731 
5732   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5733   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5734   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5735   bool legal = false;
5736 
5737   if (length > 0) {
5738     const char* p;
5739     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5740       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5741       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5742     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5743       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5744         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5745         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5746       }
5747     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5748       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5749       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5750     } else {
5751       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5752       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5753       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5754       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5755       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5756     }
5757   }
5758   if (!legal) {
5759     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5760     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5761     Exceptions::fthrow(
5762       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5763       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5764       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5765       _class_name->as_C_string()
5766     );
5767     return;
5768   }
5769 }
5770 
5771 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5772 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5773   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5774 
5775   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5776   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5777   bool legal = false;
5778 
5779   if (length > 0) {
5780     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5781       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5782         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5783         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5784       }
5785     } else {
5786       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5787       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5788     }
5789   }
5790 
5791   if (!legal) {
5792     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5793     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5794     Exceptions::fthrow(
5795       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5796       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5797       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5798       _class_name->as_C_string()
5799     );
5800     return;
5801   }
5802 }
5803 
5804 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5805 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5806   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5807 
5808   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5809   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5810   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5811   bool legal = false;
5812 
5813   if (length > 0) {
5814     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5815       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5816         legal = true;
5817       }
5818     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5819       const char* p;
5820       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5821       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5822     } else {
5823       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5824       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5825     }
5826   }
5827 
5828   if (!legal) {
5829     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5830     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5831     Exceptions::fthrow(
5832       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5833       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5834       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5835       _class_name->as_C_string()
5836     );
5837     return;
5838   }
5839 }
5840 
5841 
5842 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5843 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5844                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5845                                                    TRAPS) const {
5846   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5847 
5848   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5849   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5850   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5851 
5852   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5853     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5854   }
5855 }
5856 
5857 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5858 // Returns number of parameters
5859 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5860                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5861                                                    TRAPS) const {
5862   if (!_need_verify) {
5863     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5864     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5865     return -2;
5866   }
5867 
5868   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5869   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5870       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5871       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5872     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5873     return 0;
5874   }
5875 
5876   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5877   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5878   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5879   const char* nextp;
5880 
5881   // The first character must be a '('
5882   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5883     length--;
5884     // Skip over legal field signatures
5885     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5886     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5887       args_size++;
5888       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5889         args_size++;
5890       }
5891       length -= nextp - p;
5892       p = nextp;
5893       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5894     }
5895     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5896     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
5897       length--;
5898       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5899         // All constructor methods must return void
5900         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
5901           return args_size;
5902         }
5903         // All static init methods must return the current class
5904         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
5905             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
5906           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5907           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5908             // The actual class will be checked against current class
5909             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
5910             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
5911             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
5912             return args_size;
5913           }
5914         }
5915         // The distinction between static factory methods and
5916         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
5917         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
5918         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
5919       } else {
5920         // Now we better just have a return value
5921         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5922         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5923           return args_size;
5924         }
5925       }
5926     }
5927   }
5928   // Report error
5929   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5930   return 0;
5931 }
5932 
5933 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
5934   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5935   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
5936 }

5938 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
5939   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5940   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
5941 }
