5943 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
5944   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5945   return _field_info->_instance_size;
5946 }
5947 
5948 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
5949                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
5950   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
5951   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
5952 
5953   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
5954   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
5955   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
5956   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
5957   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
5958 
5959   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
5960     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
5961       Method* method = methods->at(j);
5962       method->init_intrinsic_id();
5963 
5964       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
5965         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
5966         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
5967         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
5968             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
5969               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
5970               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
5971               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5972               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5973             );
5974           tty->cr();
5975           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5976         }
5977         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
5978         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
5979         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
5980           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
5981             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
5982               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
5983               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5984               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5985             );
5986           tty->cr();
5987           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5988         }
5989       }
5990     } // end for
5991 
5992 #ifdef ASSERT
5993     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
5994       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
5995       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
5996       // but class C does not declare m.
5997       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
5998       // only in debug builds.
5999 
6000       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
6001         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6002           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6003           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6004           // is defined for it.
6005           continue;
6006         }
6007 
6008         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6009           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6010           // name, flags, signature.
6011           bool match = false;
6012           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6013             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6014             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6015               match = true;
6016               break;
6017             }
6018           }
6019 
6020           if (!match) {
6021             char buf[1000];
6022             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6023                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6024                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6025                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6026                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6027                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6028             );
6029             tty->cr();
6030             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6031           }
6032         }
6033       } // end for
6034     } // CheckIntrinsics
6035 #endif // ASSERT
6036   }
6037 }
6038 
6039 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook,
6040                                                       const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6041                                                       TRAPS) {
6042   if (_klass != NULL) {
6043     return _klass;
6044   }
6045 
6046   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6047     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6048 
6049   if (is_hidden()) {
6050     mangle_hidden_class_name(ik);
6051   }
6052 
6053   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, cl_inst_info, CHECK_NULL);
6054 
6055   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6056 
6057 
6058   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6059     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6060   }
6061 
6062   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6063   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6064     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6065     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6066     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6067       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6068       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6069     } else {
6070       ResourceMark rm;
6071       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6072                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6073     }
6074   }
6075 
6076   if (ik->is_value()) {
6077     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6078     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6079     vk->set_default_value(val);
6080   }
6081 
6082   return ik;
6083 }
6084 
6085 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6086 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6087 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6088 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6089 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6090 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6091 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6092 bool ClassFileParser::is_invalid_super_for_inline_type() {
6093   if (class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6094     return true;
6095   }
6096   if (is_interface() || class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6097     return false;
6098   }
6099   if (!access_flags().is_abstract() || _has_nonstatic_fields) {
6100     return true;
6101   } else {
6102     // Look at each method
6103     for (int x = 0; x < _methods->length(); x++) {
6104       const Method* const method = _methods->at(x);
6105       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6106         return true;
6107 
6108       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6109         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6110             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6111           return true;
6112         }
6113       }
6114     }
6115   }
6116   return false;
6117 }
6118 
6119 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik,
6120                                           bool changed_by_loadhook,
6121                                           const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6122                                           TRAPS) {
6123   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6124 
6125   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6126   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6127   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6128 
6129   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6130   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6131   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6132 
6133   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6134 
6135   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6136 
6137   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6138   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6139   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6140          "sanity");
6141 
6142   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6143   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6144 
6145   // Fill in information already parsed
6146   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6147 
6148   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6149   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6150   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6151   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_value()) {
6152     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6153   }
6154   if (_is_empty_inline_type) {
6155     ik->set_is_empty_inline_type();
6156   }
6157 
6158   if (this->_invalid_inline_super) {
6159     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6160   }
6161 
6162   if (_has_injected_identityObject) {
6163     ik->set_has_injected_identityObject();
6164   }
6165 
6166   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6167   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]);
6168 
6169   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6170   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6171   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6172 
6173   // can only set dynamic nest-host after static nest information is set
6174   if (cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host() != NULL) {
6175     ik->set_nest_host(cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host(), THREAD);
6176   }
6177 
6178   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6179   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6180   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6181   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6182   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6183   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6184   assert(NULL == _local_interfaces, "invariant");
6185   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6186   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6187 
6188   if (_has_final_method) {
6189     ik->set_has_final_method();
6190   }
6191 
6192   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6193   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6194   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6195   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6196   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6197   // has to be changed accordingly.
6198   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6199 
6200   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6201 
6202   if (_is_hidden || is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6203     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6204     // hidden or anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own
6205     // methods or fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6206     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is hidden or anonymous (it's
6207     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6208     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6209     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6210     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6211   }
6212 
6213   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6214   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6215   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6216   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6217   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6218     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6219   }
6220 
6221   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6222     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6223     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6224   }
6225   if (_is_hidden) {
6226     ik->set_is_hidden();
6227   }
6228 
6229   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6230   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6231   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6232   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6233   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6234 
6235   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6236   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6237   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6238 
6239   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6240 
6241   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6242   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6243     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6244   }
6245 
6246   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6247 
6248   // Miranda methods
6249   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6250       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6251       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6252         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6253      ) {
6254        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6255   }
6256 
6257   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6258   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6259   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6260   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6261 
6262   // Initialize itable offset tables
6263   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6264 
6265   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6266   // Do final class setup
6267   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6268   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6269     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6270   }
6271 
6272   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6273       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6274     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6275   }
6276 
6277   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6278   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6279 
6280   // check if this class can access its super class
6281   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6282 
6283   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6284   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6285 
6286   // check if this class overrides any final method
6287   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6288 
6289   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6290   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6291     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6292   }
6293 
6294   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6295   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6296   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6297 
6298   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6299   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6300 
6301   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6302   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6303   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6304                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6305                                  module_handle,
6306                                  _protection_domain,
6307                                  cl_inst_info.class_data(),
6308                                  CHECK);
6309 
6310   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6311 
6312   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6313   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6314   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6315     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6316                                              _all_mirandas,
6317                                              CHECK);
6318   }
6319 
6320   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6321   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6322       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6323     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6324       // We won a potential race
6325       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6326     }
6327   }
6328 
6329   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6330   if (ik->is_value()) nfields++;
6331   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6332     if (ik->field_is_flattenable(i)) {
6333       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6334       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6335       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6336       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6337           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6338           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6339       if (klass != NULL) {
6340         assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
6341         ik->set_value_field_klass(i, klass);
6342       }
6343       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6344     } else
6345       if (is_inline_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6346         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6347       ValueKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6348     }
6349   }
6350 
6351   if (is_inline_type()) {
6352     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6353     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6354       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6355       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6356       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6357     } else {
6358       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6359     }
6360     ValueKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6361   }
6362 
6363   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6364 
6365   if (!is_internal()) {
6366     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6367       ResourceMark rm;
6368       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6369       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6370     }
6371 
6372     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6373         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6374         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6375       ResourceMark rm;
6376       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6377                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6378     }
6379 
6380     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6381       ResourceMark rm;
6382       // print out the superclass.
6383       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6384       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6385         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6386                    from,
6387                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6388       }
6389       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6390       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6391       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6392         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6393         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6394           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6395           const char * to = k->external_name();
6396           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6397         }
6398       }
6399     }
6400   }
6401 
6402   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6403 
6404   // If we reach here, all is well.
6405   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6406   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6407   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6408 
6409   // it's official
6410   set_klass(ik);
6411 
6412   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6413     Universe::initialize_the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array(ik, CHECK);
6414   }
6415 
6416   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6417 }
6418 
6419 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6420   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6421   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6422 
6423   _class_name = new_class_name;
6424   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6425   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6426   // the destructor.
6427   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6428 }
6429 
6430 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6431 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6432 // its _class_name field.
6433 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6434   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6435   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6436          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6437   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6438     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6439 
6440   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6441     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6442     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6443     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6444     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6445     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6446                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6447     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6448 
6449     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6450     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6451 
6452     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6453     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6454     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6455     // when the class is unloaded.
6456     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6457   }
6458 }
6459 
6460 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6461 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6462 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6463 // exception.
6464 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6465   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6466 
6467   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6468                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6469   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6470     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6471   } else {
6472     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6473       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6474       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6475         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6476         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6477     }
6478   }
6479 }
6480 
6481 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6482   bool trusted = loader_data->is_boot_class_loader_data() ||
6483                  loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data();
6484   bool need_verify =
6485     // verifyAll
6486     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6487     // verifyRemote
6488     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6489   return !need_verify;
6490 }
6491 
6492 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6493                                  Symbol* name,
6494                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6495                                  const ClassLoadInfo* cl_info,
6496                                  Publicity pub_level,
6497                                  TRAPS) :
6498   _stream(stream),
6499   _class_name(NULL),
6500   _loader_data(loader_data),
6501   _unsafe_anonymous_host(cl_info->unsafe_anonymous_host()),
6502   _cp_patches(cl_info->cp_patches()),
6503   _is_hidden(cl_info->is_hidden()),
6504   _can_access_vm_annotations(cl_info->can_access_vm_annotations()),
6505   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6506   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6507   _orig_cp_size(0),
6508   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6509   _super_klass(),
6510   _cp(NULL),
6511   _fields(NULL),
6512   _methods(NULL),
6513   _inner_classes(NULL),
6514   _nest_members(NULL),
6515   _nest_host(0),
6516   _record_components(NULL),
6517   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6518   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6519   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6520   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6521   _class_annotations(NULL),
6522   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6523   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6524   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6525   _klass(NULL),
6526   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6527   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6528   _fac(NULL),
6529   _field_info(NULL),
6530   _method_ordering(NULL),
6531   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6532   _vtable_size(0),
6533   _itable_size(0),
6534   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6535   _rt(REF_NONE),
6536   _protection_domain(cl_info->protection_domain()),
6537   _access_flags(),
6538   _pub_level(pub_level),
6539   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6540   _synthetic_flag(false),
6541   _sde_length(false),
6542   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6543   _sourcefile_index(0),
6544   _generic_signature_index(0),
6545   _major_version(0),
6546   _minor_version(0),
6547   _this_class_index(0),
6548   _super_class_index(0),
6549   _itfs_len(0),
6550   _java_fields_count(0),
6551   _need_verify(false),
6552   _relax_verify(false),
6553   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6554   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6555   _has_final_method(false),
6556   _has_contended_fields(false),
6557   _has_flattenable_fields(false),
6558   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6559   _is_empty_inline_type(false),
6560   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6561   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6562   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6563   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6564   _implements_identityObject(false),
6565   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6566   _has_finalizer(false),
6567   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6568   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6569   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6570 
6571   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6572   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6573 
6574   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6575   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6576   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6577   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6578   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6579   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6580   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6581 
6582   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6583   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6584     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6585     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6586     // for those classes.
6587     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6588                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6589   }
6590   else {
6591     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6592                                                stream->need_verify());
6593   }
6594   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6595     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6596     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6597       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6598         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6599         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6600           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6601           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6602           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6603           // calls patch_class().
6604           //
6605           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6606           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6607           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6608           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6609         }
6610       }
6611     }
6612   }
6613 
6614   // synch back verification state to stream
6615   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6616 
6617   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6618   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6619   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6620 
6621   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6622 
6623   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6624 }
6625 
6626 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6627   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6628   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6629   _cp = NULL;
6630   _fields = NULL;
6631   _methods = NULL;
6632   _inner_classes = NULL;
6633   _nest_members = NULL;
6634   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6635   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6636   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6637   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6638   _record_components = NULL;
6639 }
6640 
6641 // Destructor to clean up
6642 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6643   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6644 
6645   if (_cp != NULL) {
6646     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6647   }
6648   if (_fields != NULL) {
6649     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6650   }
6651 
6652   if (_methods != NULL) {
6653     // Free methods
6654     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6655   }
6656 
6657   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6658   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6659     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6660   }
6661 
6662   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6663     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6664   }
6665 
6666   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6667     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6668   }
6669 
6670   // Free interfaces
6671   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6672                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6673 
6674   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6675     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6676     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6677 
6678     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6679     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6680 
6681     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6682     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6683     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6684     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6685     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6686     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6687   } else {
6688     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6689     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6690     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6691     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6692     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6693     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6694   }
6695 
6696   clear_class_metadata();
6697   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6698 
6699   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6700   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6701   // at a safepoint.
6702   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6703     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6704   }
6705 }
6706 
6707 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6708                                    TRAPS) {
6709 
6710   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6711   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6712 
6713   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6714   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6715   // Magic value
6716   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6717   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6718                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6719                      magic, CHECK);
6720 
6721   // Version numbers
6722   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6723   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6724 
6725   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6726     ResourceMark rm;
6727     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6728             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6729     Exceptions::fthrow(
6730       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6731       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6732       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6733       _major_version,
6734       _minor_version);
6735   }
6736 
6737   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6738   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6739 
6740   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6741   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6742 
6743   guarantee_property(
6744     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6745     cp_size, CHECK);
6746 
6747   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6748   if (is_hidden()) { // Add a slot for hidden class name.
6749     assert(_max_num_patched_klasses == 0, "Sanity check");
6750     cp_size++;
6751   } else {
6752     if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6753       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6754     }
6755     cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6756   }
6757 
6758   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6759                                cp_size,
6760                                CHECK);
6761 
6762   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6763 
6764   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6765 
6766   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6767 
6768   // ACCESS FLAGS
6769   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6770 
6771   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6772   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6773   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6774     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6775   }
6776   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6777   if (supports_inline_types()) {
6778     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6779   }
6780 
6781   // Access flags
6782   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6783 
6784   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6785     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6786     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6787   }
6788 
6789   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6790 
6791   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6792   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6793     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6794     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6795     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6796   }
6797 
6798   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6799 
6800   // This class and superclass
6801   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6802   check_property(
6803     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6804       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6805     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6806     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6807 
6808   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6809   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6810 
6811   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6812   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6813   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6814   if (_need_verify) {
6815     guarantee_property(class_name_in_cp->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6816                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6817                        CHECK);
6818   }
6819 
6820 #ifdef ASSERT
6821   // Basic sanity checks
6822   assert(!(_is_hidden && (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL)), "mutually exclusive variants");
6823 
6824   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6825     assert(_class_name == vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "A named anonymous class???");
6826   }
6827   if (_is_hidden) {
6828     assert(_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "hidden classes should have a special name");
6829   }
6830 #endif
6831 
6832   // Update the _class_name as needed depending on whether this is a named,
6833   // un-named, hidden or unsafe-anonymous class.
6834 
6835   if (_is_hidden) {
6836     assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
6837 #ifdef ASSERT
6838     if (_need_verify) {
6839       verify_legal_class_name(_class_name, CHECK);
6840     }
6841 #endif
6842 
6843   // NOTE: !_is_hidden does not imply "findable" as it could be an old-style
6844   //       "hidden" unsafe-anonymous class
6845 
6846   // If this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it is in the unnamed
6847   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6848   // its host class.
6849   } else if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6850     update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6851     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6852 
6853   } else {
6854     // Check if name in class file matches given name
6855     if (_class_name != class_name_in_cp) {
6856       if (_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name()) {
6857         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6858         Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6859                            vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6860                            "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6861                            class_name_in_cp->as_C_string(),
6862                            _class_name->as_C_string()
6863                            );
6864         return;
6865       } else {
6866         // The class name was not known by the caller so we set it from
6867         // the value in the CP.
6868         update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6869       }
6870       // else nothing to do: the expected class name matches what is in the CP
6871     }
6872   }
6873 
6874   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6875   // asserts that that's the case.
6876   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6877 
6878   if (!is_internal()) {
6879     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6880     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6881       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6882       LogStream ls(lt);
6883       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6884       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6885         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6886       }
6887       ls.cr();
6888     }
6889 
6890 #if INCLUDE_CDS
6891     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
6892       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
6893         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
6894         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
6895       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
6896                  !_is_hidden &&
6897                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
6898         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
6899         // Hidden and unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
6900         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
6901         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6902         bool skip = false;
6903         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
6904           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
6905           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
6906           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6907           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
6908             skip = true;
6909           }
6910 
6911           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
6912             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
6913             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6914             skip = false;
6915           }
6916         }
6917         if (skip) {
6918           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
6919             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
6920         } else {
6921           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
6922           classlist_file->flush();
6923         }
6924       }
6925     }
6926 #endif
6927   }
6928 
6929   // SUPERKLASS
6930   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6931   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
6932                                    _super_class_index,
6933                                    _need_verify,
6934                                    CHECK);
6935 
6936   // Interfaces
6937   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
6938   parse_interfaces(stream,
6939                    _itfs_len,
6940                    cp,
6941                    is_inline_type(),
6942                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6943                    &_is_declared_atomic,
6944                    CHECK);
6945 
6946   assert(_temp_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
6947 
6948   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
6949   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
6950   parse_fields(stream,
6951                is_interface(),
6952                is_inline_type(),
6953                _fac,
6954                cp,
6955                cp_size,
6956                &_java_fields_count,
6957                CHECK);
6958 
6959   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
6960 
6961   // Methods
6962   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
6963   parse_methods(stream,
6964                 is_interface(),
6965                 is_inline_type(),
6966                 &promoted_flags,
6967                 &_has_final_method,
6968                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6969                 CHECK);
6970 
6971   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
6972 
6973   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
6974   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
6975 
6976   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6977     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6978   }
6979 
6980   // Additional attributes/annotations
6981   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
6982   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
6983 
6984   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
6985 
6986   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
6987   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
6988   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
6989 
6990   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
6991   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
6992                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
6993                      CHECK);
6994 
6995   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
6996 }
6997 
6998 void ClassFileParser::mangle_hidden_class_name(InstanceKlass* const ik) {
6999   ResourceMark rm;
7000   // Construct hidden name from _class_name, "+", and &ik. Note that we can't
7001   // use a '/' because that confuses finding the class's package.  Also, can't
7002   // use an illegal char such as ';' because that causes serialization issues
7003   // and issues with hidden classes that create their own hidden classes.
7004   char addr_buf[20];
7005   jio_snprintf(addr_buf, 20, INTPTR_FORMAT, p2i(ik));
7006   size_t new_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length() + 2 + strlen(addr_buf);
7007   char* new_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, new_name_len);
7008   jio_snprintf(new_name, new_name_len, "%s+%s",
7009                _class_name->as_C_string(), addr_buf);
7010   update_class_name(SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_name));
7011 
7012   // Add a Utf8 entry containing the hidden name.
7013   assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
7014   int hidden_index = _orig_cp_size; // this is an extra slot we added
7015   _cp->symbol_at_put(hidden_index, _class_name);
7016 
7017   // Update this_class_index's slot in the constant pool with the new Utf8 entry.
7018   // We have to update the resolved_klass_index and the name_index together
7019   // so extract the existing resolved_klass_index first.
7020   CPKlassSlot cp_klass_slot = _cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index);
7021   int resolved_klass_index = cp_klass_slot.resolved_klass_index();
7022   _cp->unresolved_klass_at_put(_this_class_index, hidden_index, resolved_klass_index);
7023   assert(_cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index).name_index() == _orig_cp_size,
7024          "Bad name_index");
7025 }
7026 
7027 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
7028                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
7029                                                  TRAPS) {
7030   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
7031   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
7032   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
7033   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
7034 
7035   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
7036     check_property(_temp_local_interfaces->length() == 0,
7037         "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
7038         CHECK);
7039   }
7040   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
7041   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
7042     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
7043     if (is_interface()) {
7044       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
7045       // errors not checked yet.
7046       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
7047         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
7048         CHECK);
7049     }
7050     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7051     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
7052                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
7053                                                                super_class_name,
7054                                                                loader,
7055                                                                _protection_domain,
7056                                                                true,
7057                                                                CHECK);
7058   }
7059 
7060   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
7061     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
7062       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
7063     }
7064     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
7065       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7066     }
7067 
7068     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
7069       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7070       Exceptions::fthrow(
7071         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7072         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7073         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
7074         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7075         _super_klass->external_name()
7076       );
7077       return;
7078     }
7079 
7080     // Make sure super class is not final
7081     if (_super_klass->is_final()) {
7082       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(), "Cannot inherit from final class");
7083     }
7084 
7085     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
7086     // are acceptable super classes.
7087     if (is_inline_type()) {
7088       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
7089       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
7090         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7091         Exceptions::fthrow(
7092           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7093           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7094           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7095           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7096           _super_klass->external_name());
7097         return;
7098       }
7099     }
7100   }
7101 
7102   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7103     // This is the original source of this condition.
7104     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7105     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7106   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7107     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7108     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7109     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7110       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7111     }
7112   }
7113 
7114   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
7115   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
7116   // returns true
7117   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
7118       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
7119       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()) {
7120     set_invalid_inline_super();
7121   }
7122 
7123   if (!is_inline_type() && invalid_inline_super() && (_super_klass == NULL || !_super_klass->invalid_inline_super())
7124       && !_implements_identityObject && class_name() != vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
7125     _temp_local_interfaces->append(SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass());
7126     _has_injected_identityObject = true;
7127   }
7128   int itfs_len = _temp_local_interfaces->length();
7129   if (itfs_len == 0) {
7130     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
7131   } else if (itfs_len == 1 && _temp_local_interfaces->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
7132     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
7133   } else {
7134     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
7135     for (int i = 0; i < itfs_len; i++) {
7136       _local_interfaces->at_put(i, _temp_local_interfaces->at(i));
7137     }
7138   }
7139   _temp_local_interfaces = NULL;
7140   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7141 
7142   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7143   _transitive_interfaces =
7144     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7145                                   _local_interfaces,
7146                                   _loader_data,
7147                                   CHECK);
7148 
7149   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7150 
7151   // sort methods
7152   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7153 
7154   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7155 
7156   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7157   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7158                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7159                                                     _all_mirandas,
7160                                                     _super_klass,
7161                                                     _methods,
7162                                                     _access_flags,
7163                                                     _major_version,
7164                                                     loader,
7165                                                     _class_name,
7166                                                     _local_interfaces,
7167                                                     CHECK);
7168 
7169   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7170   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7171     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7172 
7173   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7174   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7175 
7176 
7177   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7178     if (fs.is_flattenable() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7179       // Pre-load value class
7180       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
7181           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7182           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7183       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7184       assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
7185       _has_flattenable_fields = true;
7186     }
7187   }
7188 
7189   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7190   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7191     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7192         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_inline_type(),
7193         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7194     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7195     if (is_inline_type()) {
7196       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7197       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7198       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7199     }
7200   } else {
7201     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7202   }

7203 
7204   // Compute reference type
7205   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7206 }
7207 
7208 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7209 
7210 #ifdef ASSERT
7211   if (klass != NULL) {
7212     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7213   }
7214 #endif
7215 
7216   _klass = klass;
7217 }
7218 
7219 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7220 
7221 #ifdef ASSERT
7222   if (klass != NULL) {
7223     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7224   }
7225 #endif
7226 
7227   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7228 }
7229 
7230 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7231 // clone stream with rewound position
7232 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7233   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7234 
7235   return _stream->clone();
7236 }
7237 
7238 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7239 // debugging
7240 
7241 #ifdef ASSERT
7242 
7243 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7244 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7245   if (class_name != NULL) {
7246     ResourceMark rm;
7247     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7248     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7249   } else {
7250     return true;
7251   }
7252 }
7253 
7254 #endif
